### APIInteraction

https://discord.com/developers/docs/interactions/receiving-and-responding#interaction-object

  <code className="text-sm">id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the interaction



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">application_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

ID of the application this interaction is for



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">type</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"InteractionType"}</code>
</div>

The type of interaction



</div>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">data</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIChatInputApplicationCommandInteractionData | APIMessageApplicationCommandInteractionData | ... 9 more ... | APIMessageUserSelectInteractionData"}</code>
</div>

The command data payload



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIPartialInteractionGuild"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">member</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIInteractionGuildMember"}</code>
</div>

Guild member data for the invoking user, including permissions

**This is only sent when an interaction is invoked in a guild**



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">user</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIUser"}</code>
</div>

User object for the invoking user, if invoked in a DM



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">token</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

A continuation token for responding to the interaction



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">version</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"1"}</code>
</div>

Read-only property, always `1`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">message</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessage"}</code>
</div>

For components, the message they were attached to



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">app_permissions</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Bitwise set of permissions the app or bot has within the channel the interaction was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_locale</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | \"ru\" | ... 6 more ... | \"vi\""}</code>
</div>

The guild's preferred locale, if invoked in a guild



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">entitlements</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIEntitlement[]"}</code>
</div>

For monetized apps, any entitlements for the invoking user, representing access to premium SKUs



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">authorizing_integration_owners</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIAuthorizingIntegrationOwnersMap"}</code>
</div>

Mapping of installation contexts that the interaction was authorized for to related user or guild IDs.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">context</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"InteractionContextType"}</code>
</div>

Context where the interaction was triggered from



</div></div>

### APIApplicationCommand

https://discord.com/developers/docs/interactions/application-commands#application-command-object

<div className='*:border-b [&>*:last-child]:border-b-0'><div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Unique id of the command



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">type</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"ApplicationCommandType"}</code>
</div>

Type of the command



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">application_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Unique id of the parent application



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Guild id of the command, if not global



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">name</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

1-32 character name; `CHAT_INPUT` command names must be all lowercase matching `^[-_\p&lbrace;L&rbrace;\p&lbrace;N&rbrace;\p&lbrace;sc=Deva&rbrace;\p&lbrace;sc=Thai&rbrace;]&lbrace;1,32&rbrace;$`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">name_localizations</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Partial<Record<\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | ... 7 more ... | \"vi\", string | null>>"}</code>
</div>

Localization dictionary for the name field. Values follow the same restrictions as name



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">name_localized</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The localized name



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">description</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

1-100 character description for `CHAT_INPUT` commands, empty string for `USER` and `MESSAGE` commands



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">description_localizations</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Partial<Record<\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | ... 7 more ... | \"vi\", string | null>>"}</code>
</div>

Localization dictionary for the description field. Values follow the same restrictions as description



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">description_localized</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The localized description



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">options</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIApplicationCommandOption[]"}</code>
</div>

The parameters for the `CHAT_INPUT` command, max 25



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">default_member_permissions</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Set of permissions represented as a bitset



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">nsfw</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

Indicates whether the command is age-restricted, defaults to `false`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">integration_types</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"ApplicationIntegrationType[]"}</code>
</div>

Installation context(s) where the command is available, only for globally-scoped commands. Defaults to `GUILD_INSTALL ([0])`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">contexts</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"InteractionContextType[]"}</code>
</div>

Interaction context(s) where the command can be used, only for globally-scoped commands. By default, all interaction context types included for new commands `[0,1,2]`.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">version</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Autoincrementing version identifier updated during substantial record changes



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">handler</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"EntryPointCommandHandlerType"}</code>
</div>

Determines whether the interaction is handled by the app's interactions handler or by Discord



</div></div>

### ApplicationCommandType

https://discord.com/developers/docs/interactions/receiving-and-responding#interaction-object

</div>

</div>

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

</div>

The type of interaction

  <code className="text-sm">data</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Data"}</code>
</div>

The command data payload



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIPartialInteractionGuild"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_id</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

The guild it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">channel</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"Partial<APIChannel> & Pick<APIChannel, \"id\" | \"type\">"}</code>
</div>

The channel it was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">member</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIInteractionGuildMember"}</code>
</div>

Guild member data for the invoking user, including permissions

**This is only sent when an interaction is invoked in a guild**



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">user</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIUser"}</code>
</div>

User object for the invoking user, if invoked in a DM



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">token</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

A continuation token for responding to the interaction



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">version</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"1"}</code>
</div>

Read-only property, always `1`



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">message</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIMessage"}</code>
</div>

For components, the message they were attached to



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">app_permissions</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Bitwise set of permissions the app or bot has within the channel the interaction was sent from



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">locale</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | \"ru\" | ... 6 more ... | \"vi\""}</code>
</div>

The selected language of the invoking user



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">guild_locale</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"\"id\" | \"en-US\" | \"en-GB\" | \"bg\" | \"zh-CN\" | \"zh-TW\" | \"hr\" | \"cs\" | \"da\" | \"nl\" | \"fi\" | \"fr\" | \"de\" | \"el\" | \"hi\" | \"hu\" | \"it\" | \"ja\" | \"ko\" | \"lt\" | \"no\" | \"pl\" | \"pt-BR\" | \"ro\" | \"ru\" | ... 6 more ... | \"vi\""}</code>
</div>

The guild's preferred locale, if invoked in a guild



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">entitlements</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIEntitlement[]"}</code>
</div>

For monetized apps, any entitlements for the invoking user, representing access to premium SKUs



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">authorizing_integration_owners</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"APIAuthorizingIntegrationOwnersMap"}</code>
</div>

Mapping of installation contexts that the interaction was authorized for to related user or guild IDs.



</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

<div className="flex flex-row items-center gap-4">
  <code className="text-sm">context</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"InteractionContextType"}</code>
</div>

Context where the interaction was triggered from



</div></div>

</div>

  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"boolean"}</code>
</div>

Whether the user has not yet passed the guild's Membership Screening requirements

- remarks:
If this field is not present, it can be assumed as `false`.

</div>
<div className='text-sm text-fd-muted-foreground py-4'>

  <code className="text-sm">communication_disabled_until</code>
  <code className="text-fd-muted-foreground">{"string"}</code>
</div>

Timestamp of when the time out will be removed; until then, they cannot interact with the guild



</div>

</div>

The data for the member's guild avatar decoration

See https://discord.com/developers/docs/resources/user#avatar-decoration-data-object

</div>

Whether the user has not yet passed the guild's Membership Screening requirements

- remarks:
If this field is not present, it can be assumed as `false`.

</div>

</div>

</div>

`true` if this is a TTS message

</div>

</div>

</div>
